    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_81687734" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/81687734" />
    <a title="Nicole Rayne" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2470739-nicole-rayne"><img alt="Nicole Rayne" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1364098251p2/2470739.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/81687734?book_show_action=true">Dec 21, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nicole Rayne" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nicole Rayne" href="/user/show/2470739-nicole-rayne">Nicole Rayne</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer81687734" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12702703787668156469">All right, the GONE Series is epic, and that fact is undeniable. Did I love LIES? Yes. Was it as good as the previous two? I'm not sure. One, I was expecting it to be a bit longer, and very disappointed when it ended so soon. Two, I really wish there had been a little more Diana and Caine moments, because they are the main reason I read these books, as pathetic as that sounds. Three, I wanted a better, more clear ending that explained a little more of what happened after Sanjit left the island a</span>
  <span id="freeText12702703787668156469" style="display:none">All right, the GONE Series is epic, and that fact is undeniable. Did I love LIES? Yes. Was it as good as the previous two? I'm not sure. One, I was expecting it to be a bit longer, and very disappointed when it ended so soon. Two, I really wish there had been a little more Diana and Caine moments, because they are the main reason I read these books, as pathetic as that sounds. Three, I wanted a better, more clear ending that explained a little more of what happened after Sanjit left the island and Caine helped Diana back up to safety. Like, what was Caine's reaction to Diana jumping? What was Penny doing all that time? I know it was quick, but I was still left really curious. Also, was there something between Diana and Sanjit? It seemed like it, but was difficult to tell. <br />On the bright side, I loved, LOVED all of Diana's scenes that were written (even though there were few) Her character definitely developed tremendously and while I miss the snarky, old Diana and hope that a little of that attitude will return to her, the new, sympathetic Diana is fun and complex. Diana was already a conflicted person in GONE and HUNGER, and I loved the way LIES added to her developing personality. I have to honestly say, flat out, that I loved the scene where she tried to kill Caine. That entire scene and the one that follows. And I'm a huge Caine fan, so for me to say that means it had to be well written. Diana knows the line between right and wrong and we see in this book that she really has strong morals. Despite the popular belief, she puts others who are good before herself and the ones who aren't good, even if she loves them. While, of course, if she had killed Caine, I would have been very upset, I gained tons of more respect for her character (if that's possible) when she was about to. And when she hit Penny...I was almost cheering for her. I do hope that Sanjit likes her, however, I think it would be very interesting for the plot. Make Caine hate him more, LOL!<br />Astrid- She was a bitch. A complete and utter bitch, in my opinion. But, at the same time, it made me like her a little more. I hate the classic, perfect, smart blonde and seeing her loose that air of superior perfection was refreshing. <br />I loved Taylor in this one. She really cracked me up in this one. Briana was hilarious as well, with the brain eating and such, but, after all, what else can you expect from Briana besides tons of comis relief? Quinn's parts were a little bland, but I do like how his character is improving. The Drake/Britney thing was intense and I loved it. The new characters added (especially Sanjit) were great. I felt terrible for Sam and hope things get a little better for him. Well, maybe not, because the terrible occurrences are what make the plot so interesting. <br />The one thing I would have liked most would have been to brig the characters together. Caine didn't really face anyone except for Zil and Sanjit and it would have been cool to see him go face to face with Drake or meet Sam again. But, other than that, I really enjoyed it and couldn't be more excited for PLAGUE!</span>
  <a data-text-id="12702703787668156469" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText9679046142395150654" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>"A path, a doorway, an escape to bliss. Not just a birthday: a rebirthday."</i>
</b><br /><br />It's been 7 months since all the adults disappeared. Gone.<br /><br />They survived hunger and have even set up a system for food and water. But a whole new set of problems have arisen.<br /><br />Orsay, the girl who sees the dreams of other people, and her sidekick, Nerezza, now claims to be able to see the dreams of those outside the FAYZ. And people are believing her. But Astrid believes that it means death. But are the kids that desperate to believe that whatever this is will set them free? Or is it all a <b>LIE</b>?<br /><br />Someone who was previously dead in the power plant battle is alive and walks among the living. What is up with this? And are the rumors about Drake, ALIVE, real? Or is it all a <b>LIE?</b><br /><br />Zil and the Human Crew, the people who hate freaks? They have teamed up with Caine to set Perdido Beach on fire. Reason? A distraction. Caine, on a suggestion by Bug, believes that there is an island that is still stocked with food and water. Is it true and are there still people living there? Or is it all a <b>LIE?</b><br /><br />This book. is. shocking. This book is darker than the past two, but it is an essential part of this series. The level of writing is even deeper than before and the level of emotion....don't get me started.<br /><br />Shocking truths will be revealed, shocking decisions made. And the biggest secret of all will be exposed: What exactly IS outside the FAYZ? Read the thrilling third installment of the Gone series to find out which are truths and which are LIES. </span>

But this was an exception. The Gone series has been on my shelf since around early 2016 and I'm glad to finally get to it.   <span id="freeText10494959438663932602" style="display:none">Finally had the time to finish this book today.<br />To be honest, I tend to read more stand-alone books over long series because it's much easier for me to take in all the details and story. But this was an exception. The Gone series has been on my shelf since around early 2016 and I'm glad to finally get to it. Lies was a good midpoint for the series as the events are getting much more complicated, which I liked. Throughout reading this book I thought more than once if I should give up on the series, but decided against it thanks to a good, juicy plot twist that definitely changed the reader's view. I'm glad that I'm nearing the end of the series, and I look forward to seeing how things turn out.<br /><br />Oh, I'm always open to good stand-alone recommendations so if you've got some you're welcome to send them my way!</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14266385945175477355">I fell in love with series awhile ago. It is such a strong series with great character development. It describes situations that are still relevant today. I'm getting geared up by re reading the series to get ready for Monster which is releasing in October. </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('WbQ/Oebulr+d5+hMlgWElP2DT7dKEmm2vaVUPGAbzrPD11UBXPoJR1aHipfsAmwrXNkGWhiTFPF/h4XJ81A4hA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('pB6WYMe/Z8ke3o9C7m4MZY28/Cv4GsVUK0fvHsNIrRk+ffxYfav4MdW+7ZmUaeTaLOa1xqqbuBPpZT7rUANbLg==')})
  }
